`codes.OutOfRange` for boundary violations (ErrGRPCCompacted, ErrGRPCFutureRev)\\n- `codes.ResourceExhausted` for quota limits (ErrGRPCNoSpace, ErrGRPCRequestTooManyRequests)\\n- `codes.Unavailable` (ErrGRPCDeadlineExceeded)\\n\\n**Error Translation Pattern:**\\netcd translates internal errors to gRPC errors using a mapping system (server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/util.go):\\n- `togRPCError()` function converts internal domain errors to pre-defined gRPC status errors\\n- Maintains mapping in `toGRPCErrorMap` from internal errors (membership, mvcc, auth, etc.) to gRPC errors\\n- Falls back Checking Pattern:**\\netcd client and proxy layers check status codes using `status.FromError()` to determine retry behavior and error handling:\\n- `client/v3/retry.go`: Checks if error is retryable based on code (e.g., unavailable, internal)\\n- `client/v3/watch.go`: Checks for FailedPrecondition to handle cancellation\\n- `client/v3/client.go`: Determines retry eligibility by checking code != Unavailable && code != Internal\\n- `server/proxy/grpcproxy/watch.go` and `lease.go`: Check for Canceled code to detect connection closure\\n\\n### Cross-Repository Patterns\\n\\n**Common Pattern:**\\n1. **Error Creation**: All three repos use `google.golang.org/grpc/status.Error()` or `.Errorf()` with specific codes\\n2. **Error Propagation**: Errors flow from business logic → gRPC handlers → transport layer\\n3. **Status Extraction**: `status.FromError()` extracts status info for inspection\\n4. **Code-Based Handling**: Switch statements on `status.Code()` determine behavior\\n5. **Translation**: Each repo handles translation differently:\\n   - Kubernetes: Uses both simple switch (CRI) and comprehensive mapping (gRPC-Gateway)\\n   - Grafana: Maps to internal backend status codes\\n   - etcd: Pre-allocates all errors with codes, maps internal errors → gRPC errors\\n\\n**Key Difference:**\\netcd's approach of pre-defining all errors in a centralized registry (rpctypes/error.go) and maintaining explicit mappings differs from Kubernetes' and Grafana's inline error creation patterns. gRPC status errors using `google.golang.org/grpc/status.Error()` and `status.Errorf()` with specific error codes:\\n- `codes.ResourceExhausted` for rate limiting function converts gRPC status codes to HTTP status codes\\n   - Maps: `codes.NotFound` → `http.StatusNotFound`, `codes.ResourceExhausted` → `http.StatusTooManyRequests`\\n   - Default: `http.StatusInternalServerError` for unknown codes\\n   - Handles special cases like `Retry-After` header for rate limiting\\n\\n2. **gRPC-Gateway** (vendor/github.com/grpc-ecosystem/grpc-gateway/v2/runtime/errors.go):\\n   - `HTTPStatusFromCode()` provides comprehensive mapping of all gRPC codes to HTTP status codes\\n   - Implements the Google RPC code mapping standard\\n   - Used in gateway handler (vendor/github.com/grpc-ecosystem/grpc-gateway/v2/runtime/handler.go)\\n\\n**Error Handling Pattern:**\\nKubernetes also extracts and checks status codes from errors using `status.FromError()` (staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/errors/errors.go) with `IsNotFound()` helper function.\\n\\n### grafana/grafana\\n\\n**Error Creation Pattern:**\\nGrafana creates gRPC status errors in authentication and authorization layers:\\n- `codes.Unauthenticated` for missing/invalid tokens (pkg/services/grpcserver/interceptors/auth.go)\\n- `codes.Unauthenticated` for invalid credentials (pkg/storage/unified/resource/grpc/authenticator.go, pkg/services/authz/zanzana/server/auth.go)\\n- `codes.NotFound` for unsupported resources (pkg/services/authz/rbac/service.go)\\n\\nAll created using `status.Error()` and `status.Errorf()` with descriptive messages.\\n\\n**Error Translation to Backend Status:**\\nGrafana converts gRPC status codes to internal backend status codes (pkg/tsdb/influxdb/fsql/fsql.go):\\n- `codes.InvalidArgument` → `backend.StatusBadRequest`\\n- `codes.PermissionDenied` → `backend.StatusForbidden`\\n- `codes.NotFound` → `backend.StatusNotFound`\\n- `codes.Unavailable` → `http.StatusServiceUnavailable`\\n- `codes.Unauthenticated` → `backend.StatusUnauthorized`\\n- Default: `backend.StatusInternal` for other codes\\n\\nThis is done by checking error status using `status.FromError()` and switching on code type.\\n\\n### etcd-io/etcd\\n\\n**Error Definition Pattern:**\\netcd defines comprehensive pre-allocated gRPC status errors (api/v3rpc/rpctypes/error.go) with specific codes:\\n- `codes.InvalidArgument` for parameter validation errors (ErrGRPCEmptyKey, ErrGRPCValueProvided)\\n- `codes.FailedPrecondition` for state constraint violations (ErrGRPCLeaseExist, ErrGRPCMemberExist)\\n- `codes.NotFound` for missing resources (ErrGRPCLeaseNotFound, ErrGRPCMemberNotFound)\\n- `codes.OutOfRange` for boundary violations (ErrGRPCCompacted, ErrGRPCFutureRev)\\n- `codes.ResourceExhausted` for quota limits (ErrGRPCNoSpace, ErrGRPCRequestTooManyRequests)\\n- `codes.Unavailable` for temporary failures (ErrGRPCNoLeader, ErrGRPCTimeout)\\n- `codes.DataLoss` for corruption (ErrGRPCCorrupt)\\n- `codes.PermissionDenied` for authorization failures (ErrGRPCPermissionDenied)\\n- `codes.Unauthenticated` for authentication failures (ErrGRPCInvalidAuthToken)\\n- `codes.Canceled` for cancellation (ErrGRPCWatchCanceled, ErrGRPCCanceled)\\n- `codes.DeadlineExceeded` for timeouts (ErrGRPCDeadlineExceeded)\\n\\n**Error Translation Pattern:**\\netcd translates internal errors to gRPC errors using a mapping system (server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/util.go):\\n- `togRPCError()` function converts internal domain errors to pre-defined gRPC status errors\\n- Maintains mapping in `toGRPCErrorMap` from internal errors (membership, mvcc, auth, etc.) to gRPC errors\\n- Falls back to `status.Error(codes.Unknown, ...)` for unmapped errors\\n- Special handling for context errors (context.Canceled → codes.Canceled, context.DeadlineExceeded → codes.DeadlineExceeded)\\n\\n**Error Checking Pattern:**\\netcd client and proxy layers check status codes using `status.FromError()` to determine retry behavior and error handling:\\n- `client/v3/retry.go`: Checks if error is retryable based on code (e.g., unavailable, internal)\\n- `client/v3/watch.go`: Checks for FailedPrecondition to handle cancellation\\n- `client/v3/client.go`: Determines retry eligibility by checking code != Unavailable && code != Internal\\n- `server/proxy/grpcproxy/watch.go` and `lease.go`: Check for Canceled code to detect connection closure\\n\\n### Cross-Repository Patterns\\n\\n**Common Pattern:**\\n1. **Error Creation**: All three repos use `google.golang.org/grpc/status.Error()` or `.Errorf()` with specific codes\\n2. **Error Propagation**: Errors flow from business logic → gRPC handlers → transport layer\\n3. **Status Extraction**: `status.FromError()` extracts status info for inspection\\n4. **Code-Based Handling**: Switch statements on `status.Code()` determine behavior\\n5. **Translation**: Each repo handles translation differently:\\n   - Kubernetes: Uses both simple switch (CRI) and comprehensive mapping (gRPC-Gateway)\\n   - Grafana: Maps to internal backend status codes\\n   - etcd: Pre-allocates all errors with codes, maps internal errors → gRPC errors\\n\\n**Key Difference:**\\netcd's approach of pre-defining all errors in a centralized registry (rpctypes/error.go) and maintaining explicit mappings differs from Kubernetes' and Grafana's inline error creation patterns. This makes etcd's error handling more consistent and easier to audit.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
